msg:During the first Spring Festival after my wife and I got married, we roughly finalized our travel plans and chose Dali among multiple destinations. After booking the flight, the most important thing is to choose the hotel. I checked a bunch of hotel guides on Xiaohongshu (I have to complain, Xiaohongshu‚Äôs reviews are basically soft-text promotions, and there are not many that can be read...) , almost all the recommendations point to the sea view B&B in Shuanglang, but the prices are too uneconomical. The more famous and popular ones are already 3,000+, and the price in the off-season is only a few hundred. . Finally, I chose Yuelianzhuang among the many inns.
Two days in advance, the hotel arranged for the butler Xiaojing to meet us, and thoughtfully provided us with a GL8 business car pick-up service. It was really refreshing that we didn't have to fight for a taxi or an express bus among the huge tourist crowd. After arriving at the hotel, Xiaojing helped carry our suitcases, and the luggage was very heavy, which made us feel very uncomfortable. But this kind of service attitude is really impressive. Daily fruits, drinks, instant noodles and all other imaginable services make people feel at home. I was originally very confused about whether to rent a car to go around Erhai Lake. Based on the hotel's attitude and service quality, I finally consulted the advice of Xiaojing and other housekeepers and chose the car rental company that the hotel cooperated with. There was no car rental charade that I had worried about before.
Later I went to Shuanglang. I sincerely felt that the environment in Shuanglang was really incomparable with Yuelianzhuang (there may be some B&Bs that are also great, but if you go to Shuanglang for a walk, you will probably understand what I mean).
To sum up, the environment of Yuelianzhuang Hotel is great. It has the design sense of a B&B and the service quality of a large luxury hotel. The service quality even far exceeds that of many luxury brands, which is very surprising. This is the biggest surprise of my trip to Yunnan

Except for the Lotus Bluestone, all other hotels were relatively large or famous hotels such as Marriott Hyatt or Puxiu. After all, there are so many small boutique hotels or B&Bs, and it is too difficult to make a choice. Unexpectedly, the one that gave us the most surprises in the end was the Lotus Bluestone Hotel.

From the moment we arrived at the parking lot, the housekeepers Xiaojiao and Xiaoli began their extremely considerate service. We had two large suitcases, and we never carried them ourselves since they came; the welcome desserts after arriving at the hotel were also very, very delicious (not the kind of cheap stuff that was too sweet); check-in was very smooth, and compared to queuing/waiting to check in at a big hotel, they helped us with the formalities while we were eating desserts on the sofa. The whole stay experience was very good.

After checking into the room, because we are sensitive to sound, Xiaojiao and Xiaoli quickly helped us upgrade to another quieter room, thank you very much üôè and they can also respond quickly to our daily life needs.

In addition, since we eat breakfast and dinner in the room, we need staff to go in and out. Every staff member who came in and out was very professional and polite. In comparison, the room service of staff from other large groups pales in comparison.

My wife and I often stay in hotels and are very picky about service, but this time the service at Yuelianzhuang Qingshi was really great, it can be said to be perfect. I will recommend friends to stay hereüòÑ
